# Sales, Marketing & Creative — Resume Bullet Bank

**8 Industries | 2,700 Target Bullets | CVArchitect**

Each bullet includes 4 variations, quantifiable metrics, ATS-friendly keywords, and `{variable}` placeholders for dynamic rendering. No em dashes. Seniority split: ~30% junior, ~45% mid, ~25% senior.

---

# 22. Marketing / Growth

**Industry ID:** `marketing-growth` | **Prefix:** `MKT` | **Target:** 450 bullets

### MKT-0001
**Role:** digital-marketer | **Theme:** paid-advertising | **Seniority:** mid | **Verb Context:** projects
**Keywords:** Google Ads, paid media, PPC campaigns, conversion tracking, digital advertising

**Scope:** paid search campaigns across {campaignCount} Google Ads accounts targeting {audienceSize}+ monthly prospects
**Result:** reducing cost per acquisition by {cpaReduction}% and increasing qualified leads by {leadIncrease}%

**Variations:**
- **A (Standard):** Managed paid search campaigns across {campaignCount} Google Ads accounts targeting {audienceSize}+ monthly prospects, reducing cost per acquisition by {cpaReduction}% and increasing qualified leads by {leadIncrease}%.
- **B (Result-first):** Achieved {cpaReduction}% lower cost per acquisition and {leadIncrease}% more qualified leads by managing paid search campaigns across {campaignCount} Google Ads accounts targeting {audienceSize}+ prospects.
- **C (Impact-led):** Delivered {leadIncrease}% higher lead volume while cutting acquisition cost by {cpaReduction}% — oversaw paid campaigns across {campaignCount} Google Ads accounts reaching {audienceSize}+ prospects.
- **D (Concise):** Managed {campaignCount} Google Ads campaigns targeting {audienceSize}+ prospects — {cpaReduction}% lower CPA, {leadIncrease}% more leads.

**Variables:**
  - `{campaignCount}`: 5 to 20, step 1 (integer)
  - `{audienceSize}`: 50000 to 300000, step 50000 (integer)
  - `{cpaReduction}`: 15 to 40, step 5 (percentage)
  - `{leadIncrease}`: 15 to 45, step 5 (percentage)

### MKT-0002

**Keywords:** email marketing, HubSpot, newsletter campaigns, subscriber engagement, marketing automation

**Variations:**
- **A (Standard):** Optimized email marketing automation workflows reaching {subscriberCount}+ subscribers across {workflowCount} lifecycle campaigns, increasing email open rates by {openRateIncrease}% and boosting click-through rates by {ctrIncrease}%.
- **B (Result-first):** Achieved {openRateIncrease}% higher email open rates and {ctrIncrease}% stronger click-through rates by optimizing automation workflows for {subscriberCount}+ subscribers across {workflowCount} campaigns.
- **C (Impact-led):** Delivered improved subscriber engagement — increased open rates by {openRateIncrease}% and CTR by {ctrIncrease}% through optimization of {workflowCount} email workflows serving {subscriberCount}+ subscribers.
- **D (Concise):** Optimized {workflowCount} email workflows for {subscriberCount}+ subscribers — {openRateIncrease}% higher opens, {ctrIncrease}% higher CTR.

**Variables:**
  - `{subscriberCount}`: 20000 to 200000, step 20000 (integer)
  - `{workflowCount}`: 5 to 20, step 1 (integer)
  - `{openRateIncrease}`: 10 to 30, step 5 (percentage)
  - `{ctrIncrease}`: 10 to 30, step 5 (percentage)
